permitted by Regulation S-T Rule&nbsp;101 (b)(7):&nbsp;</font><font size="2" face="Wingdings" style="font-size:10.0pt;">o</font></p>

</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Regulation S-T Rule&nbsp;101(b)(7)&nbsp;only
permits the submission in paper of a Form&nbsp;6-K if submitted to furnish a
report or other document that the registrant foreign private issuer must
furnish and make public under the laws of the jurisdiction in which the
registrant is incorporated, domiciled or legally organized (the registrant&#146;s &#147;home
country&#148;), or under the rules&nbsp;of the home country exchange on which the
registrant&#146;s securities are traded, as long as the report or other document is
not a press release, is not required to be and has not been distributed to the
registrant&#146;s security holders, and, if discussing a material event, has already
been the subject of a Form&nbsp;6-K submission or other Commission filing on
EDGAR.</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="right" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">EXHIBIT 1</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(All
amounts expressed in U.S. dollars unless otherwise noted)</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">AGNICO-EAGLE PROVIDES ANNUAL OPERATING GUIDANCE;<br>
DECLARES 28</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;font-weight:bold;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">TH</font></b><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;CONSECUTIVE ANNUAL CASH DIVIDEND;</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">TECHNICAL SESSION AT KING EDWARD HOTEL, TORONTO ON
DEC. 17</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Toronto (December&nbsp;16, 2009) &#151; <b>Agnico-Eagle Mines Limited</b> (&#147;Agnico-Eagle&#148;
or the &#147;Company&#148;) is pleased to announce that its Board of Directors has
approved the payment of a cash dividend of $0.18 per common share.&#160; The dividend will be paid on March&nbsp;26,
2010 to shareholders of record as of March&nbsp;12, 2010.&#160; Agnico-Eagle has now declared a cash dividend
to its shareholders for 28 consecutive years.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;As
we complete the last of our five new mines, our gold production is set to
double in 2010&#148;, said Sean Boyd, Vice Chairman and CEO.&#160; &#147;As a result, we enter 2010 with much greater
capacity to generate increased cash flow per share.&#160; We are also well positioned to continue to
grow output with a strong balance sheet, internal expansion opportunities,
improved access to drill our gold deposits and an expanded exploration focus&#148;
added Mr.&nbsp;Boyd.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Highlights of this corporate update include:</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2010 dividend of $0.18 per share.&#160; Declared a dividend for 28</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">th</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;consecutive year</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pinos Altos declared commercial as of November&nbsp;1,
2009</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Payable gold production(1)&nbsp;forecast for
2010 remains unchanged at 1.0 million to 1.1 million ounces.&#160; Total cash costs per ounce(2)&nbsp;are
expected to average $399 in 2010</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Gold production expected to average nearly
1.4 million ounces annually from 2011 to 2014 with total cash operating costs
expected to average of approximately $393 per ounce</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Exploration upside remains intact with
approximately $76 million of exploration expenditures budgeted in 2010,
comprising 300 kilometres of drilling</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1) Payable production means the quantity of a mineral produced during
a period contained in products that are sold by the Company, whether such
products are sold during the period or held as inventory at the end of the
period.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2) Total cash costs per ounce is a non-GAAP measure.&#160; For reconciliation of historical total cash
costs per ounce to production costs, as reported in the Company&#146;s historical
financial statements, please see the Company&#146;s financial statements and Form
20-F, as filed with US and Canadian securities regulators.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<div>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Analysts,
bankers, salespeople and investors are invited to attend a technical update on
the Company&#146;s mines and projects on December&nbsp;17, 2009 at the King Edward
Hotel in Toronto.&#160; The event will begin
at noon.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Via Webcast:</font></i></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A live audio webcast of the meeting will be available
on the Company&#146;s website homepage&nbsp;at <b><i style="font-weight:bold;">www.agnico-eagle.com.</i></b></font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Via Telephone:</font></i></p>

dial </font><font style="font-weight:normal;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">416-644-3415
</font></font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">or
Toll-free <font style="font-weight:normal;"><font face="Times New Roman">800-814-4860</font></font>.&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To ensure your
participation, please call approximately five minutes prior to the scheduled

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Replay
archive:</font></i></p>

passcode 4190782#.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The conference call will be replayed from
Thursday, December&nbsp;17, 2009</font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> at 1</font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:30
PM (E.S.T.) to Thursday, December&nbsp;24, 2009 11:59
PM (E.S.T.).&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The webcast along
with the presentation slides will be archived for 180 days<b><i style="font-weight:bold;">  </i></b>on
the website.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Continued Gold Production Growth At Low Cash Costs</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company is announcing its production and cost
guidance for 2010 through 2014.&#160; In 2010,
payable gold production is expected to be between 1.0 million and 1.1 million
ounces, up more than 100% from the projected level in 2009, as all of the
Company&#146;s six gold mines should be in commercial production.&#160; Total cash costs per ounce in 2010 are
expected to average approximately $399.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">With the Meadowbank commissioning underway and
start-up expected in January&nbsp;2010, and the Goldex and Creston Mascota
expansions scheduled to begin production in 2011, Agnico-Eagle is on course to
achieve gold production of nearly 1.4 million ounces annually over the period
of 2011 through 2014, with total cash costs estimated to average $393 per
ounce.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the past year there have been significant
changes in certain factors which will continue to affect Agnico-Eagle&#146;s total
cash cost per ounce going forward.&#160; For
example, the Canadian dollar and the Euro have strengthened against the US
dollar.&#160; Additionally, there has been
recent escalation in labour and shipping and transportation costs.&#160; Also, the slower than expected ramp-up at
Pinos Altos has resulted in a lower expectation for gold production in 2010 at
this mine.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Major Capital Projects Nearing Completion</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Agnico-Eagle is nearing the end of a significant
construction phase during which the Company has spent more than $2 billion
since the beginning of 2007.&#160; With most
of the mines in steady state operation, the remaining capital expenditures are
expected to be primarily for expansions.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s balance sheet is well positioned to
fund these initiatives.&#160; The cash balance
at September&nbsp;30, 2009 was approximately $240 million.&#160; Additionally, the Company had approximately
$200 million available under its credit facilities and expects to generate
significant cash flow from operations in 2010.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Capital expenditures are expected to total
approximately $463 million in 2010.&#160; This
includes $376 million at the mines, as broken out in the table below, and
approximately $50 million for capitalized pre-production development costs at
Meadowbank.&#160; To be conservative on the
start-up of Meadowbank, the Company is assuming in the forecast initial </font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following link may be pasted into a web browser
for more detailed information on the capital expenditures by project, by year.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/EstimatedCapitalExpenditures_Dec09.pdf</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2011, capital expenditures are expected to decline
to approximately $178 million.&#160; This
amount includes approximately $50 million for accelerated underground
development at Pinos Altos, Kittila and the LaRonde Extension.&#160; This accelerated development will result in
significant operational flexibility over the next couple of years.&#160; Additionally, an additional $25 million will
be spent at Meadowbank for an upgrade of the airstrip and site infrastructure.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Through 2011, the Company expects to be self-funding
as significant internal cash flow is expected to be generated from the sale of
approximately 2.3 million ounces of gold and the associated byproduct metals.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The capital expenditure budget does not include the
expected expenditures for the eventual expansions at Kittila, Meadowbank and
Pinos Altos.&#160; The studies for Meadowbank
and Pinos Altos are expected to be reviewed during 2010 while the Kittila study
is expected in early 2011.&#160; The capital
and more specific timelines will be presented following the reviews.&#160; Based on initial timelines and costs, Agnico-Eagle
expects to be able to internally fund these growth projects.</font></p>

<div>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Operational Improvements Ongoing</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The attached table presents the status of each of
the Company&#146;s mines and projects.&#160;
Significant operational improvements have been made and further
optimization is expected in 2010.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/ProjectStatusUpdate_Dec09.pdf</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">LaRonde&#146;s Solid and Steady Performance Continues</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">At the 100% owned <b>LaRonde</b>
mine in northwestern Quebec, proven and probable reserves of 5.0 million ounces
(35.8 million tonnes grading 4.3 grams per tonne (&#147;g/t&#148;)) are expected to
support a mine life through 2022.&#160; Please
see the table titled &#147;Detailed Mineral Reserve and Resource Data&#148; later in this
press release for further detail.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2010, payable gold production at LaRonde is
expected to decline to approximately 180,000 ounces, as gold grades are
scheduled to decline until 2012 when the deeper, and richer, ore of the LaRonde
Extension is accessed.&#160; From 2011 through
2014, gold production of approximately 248,000 ounces annually is expected,
reflecting these higher gold grades.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne(3)&nbsp;at LaRonde are
expected to remain approximately C$75 in 2010.&#160;
For the period of 2011 through 2014, minesite costs per tonne are
expected to average C$78, as the mine continues its good cost performance.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2010, total cash costs at LaRonde are expected to
be approximately $220 per ounce.&#160; From
2011 through 2014, total cash costs per ounce are expected to average
approximately $301 as byproduct revenues decline, largely due to lower zinc
grades at depth.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The table in the following link presents more
detailed data on the LaRonde mine, including projections of tonnes, grades,
mill recoveries, payable metal production and Canadian dollar minesite costs
per tonne.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/LaRondeOperationsForecast_Dec09.pdf</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Goldex Operating At Design Rates</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">At the 100% owned <b>Goldex</b>
mine in northwestern Quebec, proven and probable reserves are 1.6 million
ounces of gold (23.8 million tonnes grading 2.1 g/t).</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Goldex mine achieved commercial production on August&nbsp;1,
2008 and has consistently operated at and occasionally exceeded design
rates.&#160; During November&nbsp;2009, the
mill averaged throughput of approximately 7,600 tonnes per day (&#147;tpd&#148;) compared
with a design rate 6,900 tpd.&#160; The milled
grade was approximately 2.1 g/t, in line with the grades predicted in the
reserve model.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)&nbsp;Minesite costs per tonne is a non-GAAP
measure.&#160; For reconciliation of this
measure to production costs, as reported in the Company&#146;s historical financial
statements, please see the Company&#146;s financial statements and Form&nbsp;20-F,
as filed with US and Canadian securities regulators.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2010, payable gold production at Goldex is
expected to be approximately 164,000 ounces, while from 2011 through 2014, the
expected average gold production is approximately 169,000 ounces annually.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne at Goldex are expected to
be approximately C$23 in 2010.&#160; For the
period of 2011 through 2014 minesite costs per tonne are expected to average
$22, representing one of the lowest cost underground operations in the gold
industry.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2010, total cash costs at Goldex are expected to
be approximately $318 per ounce. From 2011 through 2014, total cash costs per
ounce are expected to average approximately $328.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The table in the following link presents more
detailed data on the Goldex mine, including projections of tonnes, grades, mill
recoveries, payable metal production and Canadian dollar minesite costs per
tonne.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/GoldexOperationsForecast_Dec09.pdf</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Kittila Mine Achieves Record Monthly Production in November</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The 100% owned <b>Kittila</b>
mine in northern Finland has proven and probable gold reserves of 3.2 million
ounces (21.4 million tonnes grading 4.7 g/t).</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kittila achieved record production of 14,500 ounces
of gold in the month of November, with approximately 3,100 tpd as compared to
the design rate of 3,000 tpd.&#160; Recovery
rates continue to approach design parameters and averaged approximately 76% in
November.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2010, payable gold production at Kittila is
expected to be approximately 147,000 ounces, while from 2011 through 2014 the
expected average gold production is approximately 158,000 ounces annually.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne at Kittila are expected to
be approximately &#128;49 in 2010.&#160; For the
period of 2011 through 2014 minesite costs per tonne are expected to average
&#128;53.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2010, total cash costs at Kittila are expected to
be approximately $502 per ounce. From 2011 through 2014, total cash costs per
ounce are expected to average approximately $520.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following link presents more detailed data on
the Kittila mine, including projections of tonnes, grades, mill recoveries,
payable metal production and local currency minesite cost per tonne.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/KittilaOperationsForecast_Dec09.pdf</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A scoping study is underway which is contemplating a
significantly higher production rate at Kittila.&#160; This would require an expansion of the mill
and accessing the deeper ore via a mine shaft.&#160;
The results of the study are expected to be reviewed in early 2011 as
drill results from the next few quarters will be incorporated.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Lapa Mine Undergoing Optimization</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The 100% owned <b>Lapa</b>
mine in northwestern Quebec has proven and probable gold reserves of 1.1
million ounces (3.8 million tonnes grading 8.8 g/t).</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2010, payable gold production at Lapa is expected
to be approximately 116,000 ounces, while from 2011 through 2014, the expected
average gold production is approximately 118,000 ounces annually.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne at Lapa are expected to be
approximately C$125 in 2010.&#160; For the period
of 2011 through 2014 minesite costs per tonne are expected to average C$123.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2010, total cash costs at Lapa are expected to be
approximately $506 per ounce. From 2011 through 2014, total cash costs per
ounce are expected to average $519.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following link presents more data on the Lapa
mine including projections of tonnes, grades, mill recoveries, payable metal
production and Canadian dollar minesite costs per tonne.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/LapaOperationsForecast_Dec09.pdf</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Due to ongoing issues with higher than expected ore
dilution underground, a more conservative budget has been put in place going
forward.&#160; Ore dilution is now assumed to
be 50% as compared to the previous assumption of 35%.&#160; Efforts are ongoing to improve and optimize
the mining cycle in an effort to maximize the profitability of this higher
grade orebody.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Pinos Altos Declares Commercial Production as of November&nbsp;1,
2009</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">At the 100% owned <b>Pinos
Altos</b> mine, located in the state of Chihuahua in northern Mexico,
commercial production has been declared as of November&nbsp;1, 2009. The
property has proven and probable gold reserves of 3.6 million ounces (41.8
million tonnes grading 2.7 g/t).&#160; The
property also contains a large silver reserve of over 100.0 million ounces
(from the same 41.8 million tonnes grading 74.6 g/t).</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the fourth quarter of 2009, the ramp-up at
Pinos Altos has been slower than expected due to issues commissioning the dry
tailings pressure filters.&#160; However, the
throughput in the mill is improving as a result of better performance from the
tailings filters.&#160; November&#146;s throughput
was 2,110 tpd, compared to 893 tpd in September.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2010, payable gold production at Pinos Altos is
expected to be approximately 151,000 ounces, while from 2011 through 2014, the
expected average gold production is approximately 210,000 ounces annually.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne(3)&nbsp;at Pinos Altos are
expected to be approximately $42 in 2010.&#160;
For the period of 2011 through 2014 minesite costs per tonne are
expected to average $40.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2010, total cash costs at Pinos Altos are
expected to be approximately $401 per ounce. From 2011 through 2014, total cash
costs per ounce are expected to average $263.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

to be reviewed in 2010.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Creston Mascota Expansion On Track To Commence
Production in 2011</font></i></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The 100% owned <b>Creston
Mascota</b> deposit at Pinos Altos, located approximately 10 kilometres
to the northwest of the main Santo Nino deposit, has probable gold reserves of
approximately 357,000 ounces (6.7 million tonnes grading 1.65 g/t). The
property also contains a silver reserve of 3.7 million ounces (from the same 6.7
million tonnes grading 17.1 g/t). This reserve is part of the total reserves
reported for Pinos Altos.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Construction on the Creston Mascota expansion is
well underway.&#160; Payable gold production
from Creston Mascota is expected to commence in 2011, with approximately 61,000
ounces of gold expected to be produced in that year.&#160; From 2011 through 2014 period, average gold
production is expected to be 48,000 ounces per year.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne at Creston Mascota are
expected to be approximately $16 in 2011.&#160;
For the period of 2011 through 2014 minesite costs per tonne are
expected to average $15.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2011, total cash costs at Creston Mascota are
expected to be approximately $322 per ounce. From 2011 through 2014, total cash
costs per ounce are expected to average approximately $396.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Creston Mascota is the first of a series of
satellite deposits at Pinos Altos that have the potential to incrementally add
to the production profile over the next several years.&#160; Other zones that are being explored include
the nearby Sinter, San Eligio and Cubiro zones.&#160;&#160; A scoping study on bringing the Sinter zone
into production will commence in 2010.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Meadowbank Start Up Anticipated In The First Quarter Of 2010</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Agnico-Eagle&#146;s 100% owned <b>Meadowbank</b> mine project in Nunavut has probable gold reserves
of 3.6 million ounces (32.8 million tonnes grading 3.5 grams per tonne).&#160; With a large additional gold resource, the
project remains open for expansion.&#160;
Initial gold production is anticipated in April&nbsp;2010.</font></p>

<div>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To date, the performance in the open pit has been
better than planned.&#160; By the end of
December, approximately 600,000 tonnes of ore is expected to be
stockpiled.&#160; The power plant has been
completed and the commissioning of the process plant is well underway.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2010, payable gold production at Meadowbank is
expected to be approximately 300,000 ounces, reflecting a budgeted contingency
for an extended commissioning period of three months of production.&#160; From 2011 through 2014, the expected average
gold production is approximately 407,000 ounces annually.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne at Meadowbank are expected
to be approximately C$68 in 2010.&#160; For
the period of 2011 through 2014 minesite costs per tonne are expected to
average C$65.&#160; These minesite costs are higher
than previous estimates largely due to increases in labour and shipping and
transportation costs.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2010, total cash costs at Meadowbank are expected
to be approximately $460 per ounce. From 2011 through 2014, total cash costs
per ounce are expected to average approximately $454, as grades are lower in
the later years of the mine&#146;s life.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following link presents more detailed data on
the Meadowbank mine, including projections of tonnes, grades, mill recoveries,
payable metal production and Canadian dollar minesite costs per tonne.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/MeadowbankOperationsForecast2_Dec09.pdf</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A scoping study is underway to consider an increase
in the proposed production rate at Meadowbank from 8,500 tonnes per day to
approximately 10,000 tonnes per day.&#160;
This additional production would come initially from accelerated
development of the Goose Island and Portage open pits and potentially from
underground on the southern end of the deposit via ramp access.&#160; The study is expected to be reviewed mid-year
2010.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Shareholders Can Reinvest Dividends In Shares At A Discount</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Under the Company&#146;s Dividend Reinvestment Plan,
shareholders have the opportunity to reinvest their dividends, commission-free,
in shares of Agnico-Eagle, at 95% of the Average Market Price, as calculated
under the Plan.&#160; Individual shareholders
can purchase up to $20,000 worth of the Company&#146;s shares, commission-free, at
the same price.&#160; Shareholders can obtain
details of the Plan from the Company or via the internet by copying the
following link into a browser.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">http://www.agnico-eagle.com/files/DividendReinvestmentPlan.pdf</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About Agnico-Eagle</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Agnico-Eagle
is a long established Canadian gold producer with operations located in Quebec,
Finland and Mexico and exploration and development activities in Canada,
Finland, Mexico and the United States.&#160;
Agnico-Eagle&#146;s LaRonde Mine is Canada&#146;s largest gold deposit in terms of
reserves.&#160; The Company has full exposure
to higher gold prices consistent with its policy of no forward gold sales.&#160; It has declared a cash dividend for 28
consecutive years.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Company&#146;s
Form&nbsp;20-F referred to below; that prices for gold, silver, zinc and copper
will be consistent with Agnico-Eagle&#146;s expectations; that prices for key mining
and construction supplies, including labour costs, remain consistent with
Agnico-Eagle&#146;s current expectations; that production meets expectations; that
Agnico-Eagle&#146;s current estimates of mineral reserves, mineral resources,
mineral grades and mineral recovery are accurate; that there are no material
delays in the timing for completion of ongoing development projects; and that
there are no material variations in the current tax and regulatory
environment.&#160; Many factors, known and
unknown, could cause the actual results to be materially different from those
expressed or implied by such forward-looking statements. Such risks include,
but are not limited to: the volatility of prices of gold and other metals;
uncertainty of mineral reserves, mineral resources, mineral grades and mineral
recovery estimates; uncertainty of future production, delays in equipment
delivery and installation, capital expenditures, and other costs; currency
fluctuations; financing of additional capital requirements; cost of exploration
and development programs; mining risks; risks associated with foreign
operations; governmental and environmental regulation; the volatility of the
Company&#146;s stock price; and risks associated with the Company&#146;s byproduct metal
derivative strategies. For a more detailed discussion of such risks and other
factors, see the Company&#146;s Annual Information Form&nbsp;and Annual Report on Form&nbsp;20-F
for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2008, as well as the Company&#146;s other
filings with the Canadian Securities Administrators and the U.S. Securities and
Exchange Commission (the &#147;SEC&#148;). The Company does not intend, and does not
assume any obligation, to update these forward-looking statements and
information, except as required by law. Accordingly, readers are advised not to
place undue reliance on forward-looking statements. Certain of the foregoing
statements, primarily related to projects, are based on preliminary views of
the Company with respect to, among other things, grade, tonnage, processing,
mining methods, capital costs, total cash costs, minesite costs, and location
of surface infrastructure. Actual results and final decisions may be materially
different from those currently anticipated.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Notes To Investors Regarding The Use Of Resources</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cautionary Note To Investors Concerning Estimates Of Measured
And Indicated Resources.</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press release may use the terms &#147;measured
resources&#148; and &#147;indicated resources&#148;. We advise investors that while those
terms are recognized and required by Canadian regulations, the SEC does not
recognize them. <b>Investors are cautioned not
to assume that any part or all of mineral deposits in these categories will
ever be converted into reserves</b>.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cautionary Note To Investors Concerning Estimates Of Inferred
Resources.</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press release may also use the term &#147;inferred
resources&#148;. We advise investors that while this term is recognized and required
by Canadian regulations, the SEC does not recognize it. &#147;Inferred resources&#148;
have a great amount of uncertainty as to their existence, and great uncertainty
as to their economic and legal feasibility. It cannot be assumed that all or
any part of an inferred mineral resource will ever be upgraded to a higher
category. Under Canadian rules, estimates of inferred mineral resources may not
form the basis of feasibility or pre-feasibility studies, except in rare cases.
<b>Investors are cautioned not to assume that
part or all of an inferred resource exists, or is economically or legally
mineable.</b></font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12</font></p>

<div style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Scientific And Technical Data</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Agnico-Eagle Mines Limited is reporting mineral
resource and reserve estimates in accordance with the CIM guidelines for the
estimation, classification and reporting of resources and reserves.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cautionary Note To U.S. Investors -</font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> The SEC
permits U.S. mining companies, in their filings with the SEC, to disclose only
those mineral deposits that a company can economically and legally extract or
produce. We use certain terms in this press release, such as &#147;measured&#148;, &#147;indicated&#148;,
and &#147;inferred&#148;, and &#147;resources&#148; that the SEC guidelines strictly prohibit U.S.-
registered companies from including in their filings with the SEC. U.S.
investors are urged to consider closely the disclosure in our Form&nbsp;20-F,
which may be obtained from us, or from the SEC&#146;s website at:
http://sec.gov/edgar.shtml.&#160; A &#147;final&#148; or
&#147;bankable&#148; feasibility study is required to meet the requirements to designate
reserves under Industry Guide 7.&#160;
Estimates were calculated using historic three-year average metals
prices and foreign exchange rates in accordance with the SEC Industry Guide
7.&#160; Industry Guide 7 requires the use of
prices that reflect current economic conditions at the time of reserve
determination which Staff of the SEC has interpreted to mean historic
three-year average prices.&#160; The
assumptions used for the mineral reserves and resources estimate reported by
the Company on February&nbsp;18th, 2009 were based on three-year average prices
for the period ending December&nbsp;31, 2008 of $725 per ounce gold, $13.32 per
ounce silver, $1.27 per pound zinc, $3.15 per pound copper, $0.90 per pound
lead and C$/US$, US$/Euro and MXP/US$ exchange rates of 1.09, 1.37 and 11.00,
respectively.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Canadian Securities Administrators&#146; National
Instrument 43-101 (&#147;NI 43-101&#148;) requires mining companies to disclose reserves
and resources using the subcategories of &#147;proven&#148; reserves, &#147;probable&#148;
reserves, &#147;measured&#148; resources, &#147;indicated&#148; resources and &#147;inferred&#148; resources.
Mineral resources that are not mineral reserves do not have demonstrated
economic viability.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A mineral reserve is the economically mineable part
of a measured or indicated resource demonstrated by a feasibility study. This
study must include adequate information on mining, processing, metallurgical,
economic and other relevant factors that demonstrate, at the time of reporting,
that economic extraction can be justified. A mineral reserve includes diluting
materials and allows for losses that may occur when the material is mined. A
proven mineral reserve is the economically mineable part of a measured resource
for which quantity, grade or quality, densities, shape and physical
characteristics are so well established that they can be estimated with
confidence sufficient to allow the appropriate application of technical and
economic parameters, to support production planning and evaluation of the
economic viability of the deposit. A probable mineral reserve is the
economically mineable part of an indicated mineral resource for which quantity,
grade or quality, densities, shape and physical characteristics can be
estimated with a level of confidence sufficient to allow the appropriate
application of technical and economic parameters, to support mine planning and
evaluation of the economic viability of the deposit.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A mineral resource is a concentration or occurrence
of natural, solid, inorganic or fossilized organic material in or on the Earth&#146;s
crust in such form and quantity and of such a grade or quality that it has
reasonable prospects for economic extraction. The location, quantity, grade,
geological characteristics and continuity of a mineral resource are known,
estimated or interpreted from specific geological evidence and knowledge. A
measured mineral</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">13</font></p>

<div style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='13',FILE='C:\JMS\105933\09-35649-1\task3844426\35649-1-ka-03.htm',USER='105933',CD='Dec 18 20:55 2009' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">resource is that part of a mineral resource for
which quantity, grade or quality, densities, shape and physical characteristics
can be estimated with a level of confidence sufficient to allow the appropriate
application of technical and economic parameters, to support mine planning and
evaluation of the economic viability of the deposit. The estimate is based on
detailed and reliable exploration, sampling and testing information gathered
through appropriate techniques from locations such as outcrops, trenches, pits,
workings and drill holes that are spaced closely enough to confirm both
geological and grade continuity. An indicated mineral resource is that part of
a mineral resource for which quantity, grade or quality, densities, shape and
physical characteristics can be estimated with a level of confidence sufficient
to allow the appropriate application of technical and economic parameters, to
support mine planning and evaluation of the economic viability of the deposit.
The estimate is based on detailed and reliable exploration and testing
information gathered through appropriate techniques from locations such as
outcrops, trenches, pits, workings and drill holes that are spaced closely
enough for geological and grade continuity to be reasonably assumed. An
inferred mineral resource is that part of a mineral resource for which quantity
and grade or quality can be estimated on the basis of geological evidence and
limited sampling and reasonably assumed, but not verified, geological and grade
continuity. The estimate is based on limited information and sampling gathered
through appropriate techniques from locations such as outcrops, trenches, pits,
workings and drill holes. Mineral resources that are not mineral reserves do
not have demonstrated economic viability.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Investors are cautioned not to assume that part or all of an
inferred resource exists, or is economically or legally mineable.</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A feasibility study is a comprehensive study of a
mineral deposit in which all geological, engineering, legal, operating,
economic, social, environmental and other relevant factors are considered in
sufficient detail that it could reasonably serve as the basis for a final
decision by a financial institution to finance the development of the deposit
for mineral production.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The mineral reserves presented in this disclosure
are separate from and not a portion of the mineral resources.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.4%;">
  <p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="36%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:36.36%;">

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The effective date for all of the Company&#146;s mineral
resource and reserve estimates in this press release is December&nbsp;31st,
2008. No independent verification of the data has been published. Additional
information about each of the mineral projects that is required by NI 43-101,
sections 3.2 and 3.3 and paragraphs 3.4 (a), (c)&nbsp;and (d)&nbsp;can be found
in the Technical Reports referred to above, which may be found at
www.sedar.com. Other important operating information can be found in the
Company&#146;s press release dated December&nbsp;11, 2008.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The contents of this press release have been
prepared under the supervision of, and reviewed by, Marc Legault P.Eng.,
Vice-President Project Development and a &#147;Qualified Person&#148; for the purposes of
NI 43-101.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Note Regarding Certain Measures Of Performance</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This news release presents measures including &#147;total
cash costs per ounce&#148; and &#147;minesite costs per tonne&#148; that are not recognized
measures under US GAAP.&#160; This data may
not be comparable to data</font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">  </font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">presented by
other gold producers.&#160; The Company
believes that these generally accepted industry measures are realistic
indicators of operating performance and useful for year-over-year
comparisons.&#160; However, both of these
non-GAAP measures should be considered together with other data prepared in
accordance with US GAAP, these measures, taken by themselves, are not
necessarily indicative of operating costs or cash flow measures prepared in
accordance with US GAAP.&nbsp; A reconciliation of the Company&#146;s total cash
cost per ounce and minesite cost per tonne to the most comparable financial
measures calculated and presented in accordance with US GAAP for the Company&#146;s
historical results of operations is set out in Note 1 to the financial
statements of the Company for the period ended September&nbsp;30, 2009 filed
with the Canadian securities regulators and the SEC.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
